import sys, re, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import camelot
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

def _clean(t): return re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', str(t)).strip()
def _split(c): return [s.strip() for s in str(c).split('\n') if s.strip()]
def _parse_num(text):
    t = _clean(text)
    if not t or t in ('-','—'): return None
    if re.match(r'^\([\d,]+\)$', t): return -float(t[1:-1].replace(',',''))
    if re.match(r'^-?[\d,]+(?:\.\d+)?$', t): return float(t.replace(',',''))
    m = re.search(r'\([\d,]+\)|[\d,]+', t)
    if m:
        raw = m.group()
        return -float(raw[1:-1].replace(',','')) if raw.startswith('(') else float(raw.replace(',',''))
    return None

dfs = camelot.read_pdf('Project_information/pr0515en-3-03.pdf', pages='34', flavor='lattice', suppress_stdout=True)
df = dfs[0].df
print('Shape:', df.shape)

ri = 2  # data row
print('=== ALL CELLS row 2 ===')
for ci in range(df.shape[1]):
    raw = str(df.iloc[ri, ci])
    items = _split(raw)
    parsed = [_parse_num(v) for v in items]
    print(f'col{ci} ({len(items)} items): {items[:5]}')
    if len(items) > 5: print(f'  ... {items[5:]}')

# find value 8039836 anywhere
print('\n=== Search for 8039836 (Money held in trust 2026) ===')
for r in range(len(df)):
    for c in range(df.shape[1]):
        if '8,039,836' in str(df.iloc[r,c]) or '8039836' in str(df.iloc[r,c]):
            print(f'  Found at row={r} col={c}: {_clean(str(df.iloc[r,c]))[:80]}')

print('\n=== Search for 11,837 (Agency accounts 2026) ===')
for r in range(len(df)):
    for c in range(df.shape[1]):
        if '11,837' in str(df.iloc[r,c]):
            print(f'  Found at row={r} col={c}: {_clean(str(df.iloc[r,c]))[:80]}')

print('\n=== col3 items (liabilities col0) ===')
items = _split(str(df.iloc[2, 3]))
print(f'{len(items)} items: {items[:10]}')
print(f'  ... {items[10:]}')

import sys, re, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import fitz
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

doc = fitz.open('Project_information/pr0515en-3-03.pdf')
page = doc[33]  # page 34 (0-indexed)

# Get page dimensions
print('Page size:', page.rect)

# Get all words with coordinates: (x0, y0, x1, y1, word, block_no, line_no, word_no)
words = page.get_text('words')
print(f'Total words: {len(words)}')

# Find the 'As of March' headers to understand column x-ranges
print('\n=== Headers containing March ===')
for w in words:
    if 'march' in w[4].lower() or 'amount' in w[4].lower() or 'year' in w[4].lower():
        print(f'  x0={w[0]:.1f} x1={w[2]:.1f} y0={w[1]:.1f}: {w[4]!r}')

doc.close()

Bash Extract ASSETS 2025 and 2026 values by x-coordinate from page 34
IN
cd "D:\Projects\SIMBA-RUNBOOKS\PICQD_Runbook" && python -c "
import sys, re, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import fitz
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

def _parse_num(text):
    t = text.strip()
    if not t: return None
    if re.match(r'^\([\d,]+\)$', t): return -float(t[1:-1].replace(',',''))
    if re.match(r'^[\d,]+$', t): return float(t.replace(',',''))
    return None

doc = fitz.open('Project_information/pr0515en-3-03.pdf')
page = doc[33]  # page 34 (0-indexed)

# All words with coords
words = page.get_text('words')

# ASSETS 2025 col: Amount header x=209-239, so values x in ~190..250
# ASSETS 2026 col: Amount header x=266-296, so values x in ~250..320
# Use x0 range to isolate each value column
# Also need y > 130 (below headers)

print('=== ASSETS 2025 values (x0: 190-250, y>130) ===')
vals_2025 = []
for w in words:
    x0, y0, x1, y1, word = w[0], w[1], w[2], w[3], w[4]
    if 190 <= x0 <= 250 and y0 > 130:
        # try to build full number (consecutive words on same y)
        if re.match(r'^[\(\d]', word):
            vals_2025.append((y0, x0, word))

# Group by y (same line = same number)
from itertools import groupby
vals_2025.sort(key=lambda x: round(x[0]))
for y, grp in groupby(vals_2025, key=lambda x: round(x[0])):
    parts = sorted(grp, key=lambda x: x[1])
    num = ''.join(p[2] for p in parts)
    print(f'  y={y:.0f}: {num}  -> {_parse_num(num)}')

print()
print('=== ASSETS 2026 values (x0: 250-330, y>130) ===')
vals_2026 = []
for w in words:
    x0, y0, x1, y1, word = w[0], w[1], w[2], w[3], w[4]
    if 250 <= x0 <= 330 and y0 > 130:
        if re.match(r'^[\(\d,]', word):
            vals_2026.append((y0, x0, word))

vals_2026.sort(key=lambda x: round(x[0]))
for y, grp in groupby(vals_2026, key=lambda x: round(x[0])):
    parts = sorted(grp, key=lambda x: x[1])
    num = ''.join(p[2] for p in parts)
    print(f'  y={y:.0f}: {num}  -> {_parse_num(num)}')

doc.close()
" 2>&1

OUT
=== ASSETS 2025 values (x0: 190-250, y>130) ===
  y=147: 1,976,083  -> 1976083.0
  y=163: 30,000  -> 30000.0
  y=183: 604,914  -> 604914.0
  y=204: 23,215  -> 23215.0
  y=220: 6,460,029  -> 6460029.0
  y=232: 46,528,793  -> 46528793.0

Bash Run UCONSBS extraction, write CSV and compare with sample
IN
cd "D:\Projects\SIMBA-RUNBOOKS\PICQD_Runbook" && python -c "
import sys, re, csv, warnings
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import config, fitz, camelot
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

exec(open('test_extraction.py', encoding='utf-8').read())

SAMPLE  = Path('Project_information/PICQD_DATA_20260515.xlsx - 2025-Q4.csv')
OUT_CSV = Path('output_uconsbs.csv')

doc = fitz.open('Project_information/pr0515en-3-03.pdf')
_, unon_pg = test_unonconsbs('Project_information/pr0515en-3-03.pdf', doc)
extracted = test_uconsbs('Project_information/pr0515en-3-03.pdf', doc, start=(unon_pg or 0)+1)
doc.close()

UCONSBS_CODES = [c for c in config.COLUMN_CODES if c.startswith('PICQD.UCONSBS.')]
UCONSBS_HDRS  = [config.COLUMN_HEADERS[config.COLUMN_CODES.index(c)] for c in UCONSBS_CODES]

# write CSV
with open(OUT_CSV, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    w = csv.writer(f)
    w.writerow(['period'] + UCONSBS_CODES)
    w.writerow([''] + UCONSBS_HDRS)
    for period in sorted(extracted):
        row = [period] + [extracted[period].get(c) for c in UCONSBS_CODES]
        w.writerow(row)
print(f'CSV: {OUT_CSV}')

# compare with sample
def load_sample(path):
    if not path.exists(): return {}
    with open(path, encoding='utf-8-sig') as f:
        rows = list(csv.reader(f))
    if len(rows) < 3: return {}
    codes = rows[0]
    sample = {}
    for row in rows[2:]:
        if not row or not row[0].strip(): continue
        period = row[0].strip()
        sample[period] = {codes[i]: row[i] for i in range(len(codes)) if i < len(row)}
    return sample

sample = load_sample(SAMPLE)
ok = fail = miss = 0
for period in sorted(extracted):
    if period not in sample: print(f'{period}: not in sample'); continue
    for code in UCONSBS_CODES:
        ext_val = extracted[period].get(code)
        smp_raw = sample[period].get(code, '')
        try: smp_val = float(smp_raw.replace(',','')) if smp_raw.strip() not in ('','-','—') else None
        except: smp_val = None
        if ext_val is None and smp_val is None: miss += 1
        elif ext_val == smp_val: ok += 1
        else: fail += 1; print(f'MISMATCH {period} {code}: extracted={ext_val} sample={smp_val}')

print(f'UCONSBS: {ok} match, {fail} mismatch, {miss} both-None')

# print table
print('\n-- Extracted values --')
hdr = 'Code                                    2025-Q1        2026-Q1'
print(hdr); print('-'*60)
for code in UCONSBS_CODES:
    label = code.replace('PICQD.UCONSBS.', '')
    v1 = str(extracted.get('2025-Q1',{}).get(code,'None'))
    v2 = str(extracted.get('2026-Q1',{}).get(code,'None'))
    print(f'{label:<40} {v1:>12}   {v2:>12}')
" 2>&1

cd "D:\Projects\SIMBA-RUNBOOKS\PICQD_Runbook" && python -c "
import sys, re, csv, warnings
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import config, fitz, camelot
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
import importlib.util
spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('te', 'test_extraction.py')
te = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(te)

Q4_PDF = 'Project_information/sample/pr0213en-03.pdf'
doc = fitz.open(Q4_PDF)
print(f'PDF: {Q4_PDF}  ({len(doc)} pages)')

# Period detection
cur_period = None
for pg in range(min(3, len(doc))):
    txt = doc[pg].get_text('text')
    m = re.search(r'(?:Fiscal Year|(?:Three|Six|Nine) Months) Ended (\w+) \d{1,2}, (\d{4})', txt, re.I)
    if m:
        months = {'january':1,'february':2,'march':3,'april':4,'may':5,'june':6,'july':7,'august':8,'september':9,'october':10,'november':11,'december':12}
        mn = months.get(m.group(1).lower(), 0)
        q = config.MONTH_TO_QUARTER.get(mn, 0)
        cur_period = f'{m.group(2)}-Q{q}'; break
print(f'Current period: {cur_period}')

# Test UNONCONSBS
r_unon, unon_pg = te.test_unonconsbs(Q4_PDF, doc)

# Test UCONSBS
r_ucons = te.test_uconsbs(Q4_PDF, doc, start=(unon_pg or 0)+1)

doc.close()

# Write CSV with both tables
CODES = [c for c in config.COLUMN_CODES if c.startswith('PICQD.UNONCONSBS.') or c.startswith('PICQD.UCONSBS.')]
HDRS  = [config.COLUMN_HEADERS[config.COLUMN_CODES.index(c)] for c in CODES]

all_results = {}
for p, d in r_unon.items():   all_results.setdefault(p, {}).update(d)
for p, d in r_ucons.items():  all_results.setdefault(p, {}).update(d)

with open('output_q4_bs.csv', 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    w = csv.writer(f)
    w.writerow(['period'] + CODES)
    w.writerow([''] + HDRS)
    for period in sorted(all_results):
        row = [period] + [all_results[period].get(c) for c in CODES]
        w.writerow(row)

print()
print('-- UNONCONSBS extracted values (vs expected) --')
exp_unon = {
    'PICQD.UNONCONSBS.ASSET.CASHDEP.Q':    {'2025-Q1': 1970343, '2025-Q4': 1510713},
    'PICQD.UNONCONSBS.ASSET.CALLOAN.Q':    {'2025-Q1': 30000,   '2025-Q4': 30000},
    'PICQD.UNONCONSBS.ASSET.MONHELD.Q':    {'2025-Q1': 6460029, '2025-Q4': 7815229},
    'PICQD.UNONCONSBS.ASSET.SEC.Q':        {'2025-Q1': 46528662,'2025-Q4': 45548052},
    'PICQD.UNONCONSBS.ASSET.SEC.JGOVBOND.Q':{'2025-Q1': 35390389,'2025-Q4': 34418337},
    'PICQD.UNONCONSBS.ASSET.TOTAL.Q':      {'2025-Q1': 59555517,'2025-Q4': 58977410},
}
for code, exp in exp_unon.items():
    label = code.replace('PICQD.UNONCONSBS.','')
    for p in sorted(all_results):
        got = all_results[p].get(code)
        e   = exp.get(p, '?')
        ok  = 'OK' if got == e else f'FAIL(expected {e})'
        print(f'  {label:<35} {p}: got={got}  {ok}')

print()
print('-- UCONSBS extracted values (vs expected) --')
exp_ucon = {
    'PICQD.UCONSBS.ASSET.CASHDEP.Q':       {'2025-Q1': 1976083, '2025-Q4': 1514519},
    'PICQD.UCONSBS.ASSET.MONHELD.Q':       {'2025-Q1': 6460029, '2025-Q4': 7815229},
    'PICQD.UCONSBS.ASSET.SEC.Q':           {'2025-Q1': 46528793,'2025-Q4': 45547815},
    'PICQD.UCONSBS.ASSET.TANFIX.LAND.Q':   {'2025-Q1': 76632,   '2025-Q4': None},
    'PICQD.UCONSBS.ASSET.TOTAL.Q':         {'2025-Q1': 59555692,'2025-Q4': 58975295},
}
for code, exp in exp_ucon.items():
    label = code.replace('PICQD.UCONSBS.','')
    for p in sorted(all_results):
        got = all_results[p].get(code)
        e   = exp.get(p, '?')
        ok  = 'OK' if got == e else f'FAIL(expected {e})'
        print(f'  {label:<35} {p}: got={got}  {ok}')

print('\nCSV: output_q4_bs.csv')

import fitz, re, warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

doc = fitz.open('Project_information/sample/pr0213en-03.pdf')
page = doc[14]  # page 15 (0-indexed) = UCONSBS

words = page.get_text('words')
print('=== Header words (y < 160) ===')
for w in sorted(words, key=lambda x: x[1]):
    if w[1] < 160:
        print(f'  x0={w[0]:.1f} y0={w[1]:.1f}: {w[4]!r}')

print()
print('=== Amount words ===')
for w in words:
    if 'amount' in w[4].lower():
        print(f'  x0={w[0]:.1f} y0={w[1]:.1f}: {w[4]!r}')

doc.close()

import camelot, warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

def _clean(t): 
    import re; return re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', str(t)).strip()
def _split(c): return [s.strip() for s in str(c).split('\n') if s.strip()]

# Q4 UNONCONSBS page 7, both lattice and stream
print('='*60)
print('Q4 UNONCONSBS p7 - LATTICE')
print('='*60)
tbls = camelot.read_pdf('Project_information/sample/pr0213en-03.pdf', pages='7', flavor='lattice', suppress_stdout=True)
print(f'Tables found: {len(tbls)}')
for i, t in enumerate(tbls):
    df = t.df
    print(f'  Table {i}: shape={df.shape}')
    for ri in range(min(4, len(df))):
        for ci in range(df.shape[1]):
            items = _split(str(df.iloc[ri,ci]))
            if items: print(f'    r{ri}c{ci} ({len(items)}): {items[:4]}')

print()
print('='*60)
print('Q4 UNONCONSBS p7 - STREAM')
print('='*60)
tbls = camelot.read_pdf('Project_information/sample/pr0213en-03.pdf', pages='7', flavor='stream', suppress_stdout=True)
print(f'Tables found: {len(tbls)}')
for i, t in enumerate(tbls):
    df = t.df
    print(f'  Table {i}: shape={df.shape}')
    for ri in range(min(5, len(df))):
        for ci in range(df.shape[1]):
            items = _split(str(df.iloc[ri,ci]))
            if items: print(f'    r{ri}c{ci}: {items[:3]}')

Bash Extract Q4 UNONCONSBS and UCONSBS tables via both lattice and stream camelot to text
IN
cd "D:/Projects/SIMBA-RUNBOOKS/PICQD_Runbook" && python -c "
import camelot, warnings, sys
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
pdf = 'Project_information/sample/pr0213en-03.pdf'

for pg, label in [(7,'UNONCONSBS'), (15,'UCONSBS')]:
    print(f'=== {label} p{pg} (lattice) ===')
    tbls = camelot.read_pdf(pdf, pages=str(pg), flavor='lattice', suppress_stdout=True)
    for ti, t in enumerate(tbls):
        df = t.df
        print(f'Table {ti}: shape {df.shape}')
        for ri in range(len(df)):
            print(f'  r{ri}: {[str(df.iloc[ri,ci]) for ci in range(df.shape[1])]}')
    print()
    print(f'=== {label} p{pg} (stream) ===')
    tbls2 = camelot.read_pdf(pdf, pages=str(pg), flavor='stream', suppress_stdout=True)
    for ti, t in enumerate(tbls2):
        df = t.df
        print(f'Table {ti}: shape {df.shape}')
        for ri in range(len(df)):
            print(f'  r{ri}: {[str(df.iloc[ri,ci]) for ci in range(df.shape[1])]}')
    print()
